msg:I like hotels with courtyards, which is the reason why I booked Ritz-Carlton without hesitation. In fact, it is more like a castle full of artistic atmosphere. The European-style decoration is matched with the celadon style. It is bright and elegant. The corridor is covered with light brown pattern wallpaper, and the aisle is decorated with elegant landscape paintings and figure paintings. It is pleasing to the eye.
üåàThe location is super good: near the Haihe Daguangming Bridge, a few steps to the riverside, the center of the former British capital, quiet in the bustling city. In front of the hotel is Victoria Garden. Going left is Jiefang North Road, the former Oriental Wall Street, the old site of major foreign banks, and now the Financial Street. The Tianjin branch of the Industrial and Agricultural Construction Bank is here, and Zhang Xueliang's former residence is also nearby; going right is Dagu North Road, from which you can go to the Porcelain House and the Italian Style District, no more than 2 kilometers away, and then go forward to the Tianjin Eye; right in front of the door is Tai'an Road, and the corner is the 12 STAY Coffee decorated with pink roses, which is suitable for punching in and taking pictures; go to the right on Tai'an Road, turn left at Zhejiang Road, and walk all the way to the Little White Building, Tianjin Concert Hall, and Wudadao, which is less than two kilometers away. In addition, Xikai Church is also nearby. In short, living here is very suitable for measuring Tianjin's ** area with your legs/small yellow car, as if wandering in a small Europe.
üåàFree parkingüÖøÔ∏è: There is a basement, convenient parking, free, and scan the code at the front desk to apply for exemption.
üåàComfortable room: The room is large, European style, elegantly decorated, and the lobby has blue and white porcelain walls. There is a desk, a coffee table, and a terrace. The terrace offers a garden view. I especially like rooms with terraces. It's a little surprise:) There is a corridor outside the room, and you can see the Haihe River from the corridor.
üåà The bathroom is spacious and easy to use: it is the design I like, with two wash basins and a bathtub on one sideüõÅ The hotel service is very good. After dragging the luggage and leading to the room, the floor attendant will immediately ask if you need to add supplies; there are 6 bottles of mineral water in the room, which is enough. There is a shower and toilet on one side. The bathroom is from TOTO, and the toiletries are from the French diptyque brand, which are of good qualityüëçThe toilet is electric, which suits my taste very well. Dyson's hair dryer, accessories are all placed on the ground for backup.
üåà Convenient charging facilities: There are 3 USB charging ports and a socket on the bedside tables on both sides, and there is a row of sockets next to the desk, which is very practical. TYPE- C head needs to bring its own plug.
üåà The breakfast is quite satisfactory: it is quite rich, with pancakes, noodles, fruits, salads, and juices.
üåàThe service is very good: Check-in is very fast, there is a special person to drag the luggage and guide to the room, and the floor attendant will immediately ask if you need to add supplies; there are 6 bottles of mineral water in the room, and the attendant will also take the initiative to give them; check-out is also very fast, because several desks are checking in, the room card is directly handed to the front desk attendant.
üåàFitness facilities: There are gyms and swimming pools, free for guests. The swimming pool is not big 25*5? But the locker room exceeded my expectations, it is very large, in addition to the shower room, sauna room (dry and wet), there is also a dressing room and a lounge chair rest area, hehe, you can also enjoy it here.
üå∏ Overall, I am very satisfied with the hotel. If I have to nitpick, there are still the following shortcomings:
üíß The drawers in the cabinet still have a smell and cannot be used;
üíß There are no paper towels on the desk/bedside in the room, which is inconvenient;
üíß British design, it would be better if it could be equipped with British tea sets;
üíß Several spotlights on the top of the bedroom are broken and have not been replaced;
üíß There is no trash can in the toilet
üíß The outdoor garden on the third floor has fewer flowers and is more like a terrace. The garden on the first floor also has less scenery. Of course, the Victorian garden outside is already a highlight.

msg:Tianjin Ritz is the hotel that has amazed me the most recently. If Nanjing Ritz is the representative of the new luxury, then Tianjin Ritz is the aristocratic hotel in the mainland that is almost unrepeatable. The hotel is a renovation of the former Gordon Hall (the former British Municipal Council and the seat of the Tianjin Municipal Government after liberation). Its historical charm far exceeds that of most luxury hotels in China. The hotel is a classic British red brick building with a magnificent style. As soon as you enter the hotel gate, you will see the Victorian castle-style lobby, which is decorated with a fusion of Western and Chinese cultural characteristics, and is extremely luxurious. The guest room floors and room layouts also show the elegant style of the Victorian era. What is particularly amazing is that the public area of ‚Äã‚ÄãTianjin Ritz can be described as a temple of art. From the lobby on the first floor to the hotel guest room floor, classic Chinese and Western paintings can be seen everywhere, which makes guests who love art extremely pleasing to the eye. The service of Tianjin Ritz is impeccable. From the doorman who takes the initiative to welcome guests and help with luggage as soon as they get off the car, to the enthusiastic and professional front desk lady, and the sweet and thoughtful concierge lady who sends guests to the room and gives a detailed introduction to the hotel, the entire check-in process is extremely smooth, and the Ritz's top service level can be felt throughout the process. Let's talk about the executive lounge. The environment here is very distinctive. The oil paintings and model decorations with the theme of the Age of Discovery, and the lounge areas with different styles of afternoon tea, dinner, and bar are unique. The executive lounge of Tianjin Ritz was once rated as the best executive lounge in the Asia-Pacific region at the third HDA. Its level can be seen. Here, you can enjoy the supreme service level of the ladies in the executive lounge with five meals a day. In addition, Ritz's health facilities are also very complete. The staff of the health center and room service are very polite and enthusiastic, giving people a sense of intimacy at home.

posted:Posted May 9, 2024
msg:The hotel's hardware facilities and external environment are really amazing. I was attracted by these. Most of the staff's attitudes are also very good, polite and enthusiastic. The hygiene is also acceptable, at least there are no obvious stains to the naked eye. The main points of dissatisfaction are as follows:
1. There is no welcome fruit or welcome refreshments. All drinks in the mini bar except mineral water are charged. I have stayed in many expensive hotels, and this is the first time I have encountered this. Of course, I also think this is a favor, not a duty, and I can understand it.
2. You need to go down and get the takeaway by yourself. There is no staff to provide food delivery service or equipped with robots. Now most fast hotels are equipped with robots for food delivery, and this is not a very labor-intensive and financial operation.
3. The staff have different opinions and rules on whether you can take pictures in the hotel. This is also what confuses me the most. My friend and I took pictures in the hotel lobby on the night of check-in. Because we wanted to take a photo of two people, we used a tripod. There were many staff in the lobby at that time, but no one stopped us or suggested that we could not use a tripod to take pictures. But when we went to the same location to continue shooting the next day, a staff member in the lobby first came up to ask if we were hotel guests (this was also outrageous, because the two of us went down from the internal elevator to the lobby on the first floor. It was more than 9 or 10 o'clock in the daytime, and there were almost no guests checking in or taking photos in the lobby. In theory, my friend and I should be very conspicuous as hotel guests). After we made it clear that we were guests, the staff member said that we could take photos, but we could not use a tripod. If we needed to take a double photo, we could ask the staff for help. Although the staff member's tone and attitude were quite gentle, we were still a little unhappy. If your hotel does not allow the use of a tripod for shooting, why didn't anyone stop us the night before? My friend and I are not unreasonable people. If we were stopped the night before, we can indeed understand that your hotel has such a requirement, and we will definitely not continue to use it the next day. But the different requirements of different staff members before and after give us reason to doubt: the staff who stopped us the next day subjectively determined that we came to the hotel to "take photos" and made things difficult for us. Although this is not a big deal, it still makes people feel very uncomfortable. I hope your hotel can strengthen staff training, or at least unify their words. Seeing that your reviews are all praising the environment and hardware, there is nothing wrong with that. So you should pay more attention to the quality of service and don't waste such good hardware conditions.

info:Premier Double Room
info:Stayed in March 2023
info:Family
info:24 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 12, 2023
msg:The Ritz-Carlton Tianjin is really luxurious

There is a nameplate on the gate
It read: "The location and architectural legend of The Ritz-Carlton, Tianjin dates back to 1890 and has profound cultural and historical significance."

Baidu a bit

This used to be the Gordon Hall of Tianjin Ministry of Industry and Commerce
However, the main building of Gordon Hall was damaged and demolished during the Tangshan Earthquake
The annex building of Gordon Hall, the former site of the British National Fire Brigade, still retains the original appearance of the building
The hotel was designed and built on the site of the original Gordon Hall, and the architectural shape draws on the architectural outline of Gordon Hall

1. Brand benefits. The hotel itself is remodeled according to the historical old buildings in Tianjin. The location is superior and travel is convenient. There is a Hisense Plaza nearby, and restaurants and supermarkets are convenient.
2. The staff is enthusiastic and will take the initiative to say hello and serve actively.
3. The breakfast is rich, and the business hours are long from 6 to 10 o'clock.
Two, other
1. No features: In recent years, light luxury hotels have risen in China, and the cost performance of old star-rated hotels has been challenged. In contrast, Atour, All Seasons, Orange, Langlizi, Lavande, Time Walk and other light luxury hotels, theme hotels, more humanized design, smarter and more fashionable, more suitable for young people to consume.
Veteran star-rated hotels such as the Ritz-Carlton still rely on traditional services. 2. Not smart enough: the room area is large and the facilities are perfect to grab customers, and the competitiveness has been weakened. Especially intelligent applications, such as robot services, smart rooms, such as voice-activated switch lights, sensors, themes, personalized decoration, etc. are not as fast as light luxury hotels. The slippers are almost as thin as those of the Express Hotel.
3. Lack of innovation: Old star-rated hotels have no innovation and are basically the same. Large rooms, various facilities, mini bars for drinks, bathtubs, etc. are more suitable for business, or people who are older and have conservative consumption concepts.
4. Not humanized enough: Not friendly enough for parent-child tours, no equipment and facilities for children, the minimum washbasin is out of reach of children, and there are no pedals. No children's slippers etc. The small snacks in the room are still the traditional routine, with a huge increase in price. No value-added fruits, snacks and other gifts.
In short, if you want to meet, you can get reimbursed, you can live in this kind of star hotel, if you want fashion, comfort and cost-effective, it is recommended to light luxury hotels.
